[2;36m                    [0m         [95mss[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m -v [0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmpwh27ubkf[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproduce ExpanderFuzzer -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run of the `ExpanderFuzzer` against the Commons Compress example [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander` utility triggered a low-severity security issue due to uncontrolled [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory allocation. Specifically, feeding a crafted testcase into the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`decompress`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`expand` logic invoked the LZW decompression code path, leading to a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`. The fuzzer reported this as a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  When `ExpanderFuzzer` invokes the example `Expander.expand` method on a specially[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted input, the Apache Commons Compress LZW decompression implementation [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocates tables whose size grows until the JVM heap is exhausted. This manifests [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas a `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`, reported by Jazzer as [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Resource exhaustion due to unbounded memory allocation. The fuzzer framework [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcategorizes it as a low-severity security issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Observations and Findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack trace identifies [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream.initializeTables` as [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe site of the heap exhaustion.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception propagates through the compressor factory [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, into `Expander.decompress`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `Expander.expand`, and ultimately ends in the fuzzer harness [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer run was configured with a [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m GB shared memory limit and default JVM [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap; the crash suggests no upper bound on decompression resource usage for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed or adversarial data.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer’s instrumentation loaded extensive coverage and sanitizer hooks across [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmany Commons Compress and Commons IO classes before the crash occurred.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas to Investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **LZWInputStream.initializeTables [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZWInputStream.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Review table allocation logic and how input parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., code size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m may [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlead to unbounded growth.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mCompressorStreamFactory.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Understand how stream wrappers delegate to specific compressor implementations[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand whether resource limits can be injected.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Expander.decompress & Expander.expand [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Examine how the example harness reads input streams, chooses compressor types,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand whether it enforces any bounds on decompressed size.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Although not the root cause, the harness entry point shows how the fuzzed data[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis passed into the library and may reveal missing safety checks or configuration [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moptions.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo root‐cause speculation or remediation steps are included here; this report [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfocuses solely on documenting the observed out-of-memory behavior and the relevant [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode paths.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m561[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mZ.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m562[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m563[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m564[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mDEFLATE.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m228[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m221[0m[39m:    private void [0m[1;35mdecompress[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString streamName, Path archive, Path [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, CompressorException [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m222[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory.getSingleton[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35m.createCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstreamName, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39marchive[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m224[0m[39m:            String fileName = [0m[32m"decompressed.bin"[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m225[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis instanceof GzipCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m226[0m[39m:                GzipParameters parameters = [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mGzipCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getMetaData[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m227[0m[39m:                fileName = [0m[1;35mparameters.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m228[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `.Z` decompression path in [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"z"[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     always passes `memoryLimitInKb == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` to `ZCompressorInputStream`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Consequently, `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskips its memory‐check[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly applied when `memoryLimitInKb > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and unconditionally allocates [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlarge tables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     leading to unbounded memory usage and eventual `OutOfMemoryError`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Overview[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a sensible default memory cap for `.Z` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLZW[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m decompression when the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfactory’s `memoryLimitInKb` is unset.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve the existing default behavior for other compressors and avoid [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreaking backward compatibility.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not touch the fuzzer harness or tests.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `CompressorStreamFactory` [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStreamFactory.java[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Define a constant for the default `.Z` memory limit, e.g.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m kb[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final int DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB = [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMiB[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Add a public setter to override the factory’s memory limit:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Sets the soft memory limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39min KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for LZW [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.Z[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m decompression.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * Must be greater than zero. By default, a safe cap [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB is used.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * @param memoryLimitInKb memory cap in KiB[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          * @return this factory for chaining[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         public CompressorStreamFactory [0m[1;35msetMemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemoryLimitInKb <= [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"memoryLimitInKb must be > 0"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             this.memoryLimitInKb = memoryLimitInKb;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return this;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Modify the `.Z` branch in `[0m[1;35mcreateCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to apply the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault limit when[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         the factory’s `memoryLimitInKb` is unset [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`<= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```diff[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mZ.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-            return new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m if user did not set a limit, fall back to a safe default[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            int effectiveLimit = memoryLimitInKb > [0m[1;36m0[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+                ? memoryLimitInKb[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+                : DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+            return new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, effectiveLimit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Update Javadoc on the factory class to mention the new default cap for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`.Z`.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. No changes to the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or test code.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch enforces a concrete upper‐bound on memory allocated by the LZW [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtables, eliminating[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     the uncontrolled allocation vulnerability.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other compressors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., XZ, LZMA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain unaffected unless users explicitly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mset `memoryLimitInKb`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By adding a setter, advanced users can still override or disable the default [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcap for legitimate large‐scale data.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Backward‐compatibility is preserved: existing code using the factory without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifications now[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     still works, but with a built‐in safe limit for `.Z`.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extreme legitimate `.Z` archives with enormous code tables [0m[1;39m([0m[39mover [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtables[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     throw a `MemoryLimitException` instead of silently exhausting the heap.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who need to process such archives can call `[0m[1;35m.setMemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe factory[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     before decompression to raise the cap.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change does not alter any fuzzer or test harness behavior and does not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodify external dependencies.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ZCompressorInputStream` constructor invokes `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint,int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` performs the actual memory check [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen `memoryLimitKiB > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `CompressorStreamFactory` is the sole creator of `ZCompressorInputStream` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin Commons Compress.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arises during fuzz testing of the `ExpanderFuzzer` target in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache Commons Compress: a Java `OutOfMemoryError` occurs inside [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.initializeTables`, triggered by unbounded memory use when [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompressing “.Z” archives. To mitigate this, a patch was proposed in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory.java` that adds a configurable soft memory cap [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`memoryLimitInKb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a default of [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB and exposes it via a setter. After [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplying the patch, the build fails with a compilation error: “cannot assign a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue to final variable memoryLimitInKb,” indicating that the newly introduced [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetter cannot modify the [0m[1;39m([0m[39mundeclared or incorrectly declared[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m `memoryLimitInKb` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfield.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzer log shows that `ExpanderFuzzer` runs into a `FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOut of memory` caused by `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.initializeTables`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace leads through `ZCompressorInputStream` and [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream`, indicating that “.Z” [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompression has no upper bound on the in-memory tables.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - libFuzzer reports a crashing input and generates a reproducer, confirming that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muncontrolled memory growth in LZW decompression is the immediate failure point.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `CompressorStreamFactory.java`, a new constant DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m64[0m[39m × [0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was added.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A new instance field `memoryLimitInKb` was introduced [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimplicitly assumed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialized to zero or default.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A public setter method `[0m[1;35msetMemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` was added, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrowing if the argument ≤ [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m and assigning to `this.memoryLimitInKb`.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the factory’s switch over compressor names, the code for `Z` now computes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man effective limit: if `memoryLimitInKb` was set [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, use it; otherwise use the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault, then passes it to `new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, effectiveLimit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Post-Patch Build Log  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compilation starts, recompiling `CompressorStreamFactory.java`.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Error: `[0m[35m/src/.../[0m[95mCompressorStreamFactory.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m454[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m13[0m[1;39m][0m[39m cannot assign a value [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto final variable memoryLimitInKb`  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The setter attempts `this.memoryLimitInKb = memoryLimitInKb;`, but [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memoryLimitInKb` was declared as `final`, preventing assignment after [0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Further Investigation  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify the declaration of the `memoryLimitInKb` field in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorStreamFactory`:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Is it declared `private final int memoryLimitInKb;`?  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Should it be non-final or assigned a default in the constructor?  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect class constructors and existing fields to determine where and how [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m442[0m[39m:     * Constructs an instance with the provided decompress Concatenated option.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m443[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m444[0m[39m:     * @param decompressUntilEOF if true, decompress until the end of the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput; if false, stop after the first stream and leave the input position to point [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStreamFactory.jav[0m[1;92ma:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m550[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m550[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mLZMACompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m551[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m552[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mPACK200.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m553[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mPack200CompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m554[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m555[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mSNAPPY_RAW.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m556[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mSnappyCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m557[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m558[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mSNAPPY_FRAMED.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m559[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mFramedSnappyCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m560[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m561[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mZ.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m562[0m[39m:                return new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, memoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m563[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m564[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mDEFLATE.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Remove `final` modifier from `memoryLimitInKb`**  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `CompressorStreamFactory.java`, change the field declaration  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m before[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private final int memoryLimitInKb;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private int memoryLimitInKb;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Rationale: The setter `[0m[1;35msetMemoryLimitInKb[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` needs to mutate this field. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemoving `final` resolves the compilation error.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Ensure all constructors initialize `memoryLimitInKb`**  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the no-arg constructor, retain `this.memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindicates [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"unset"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the single-arg constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBoolean [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompressUntilEOF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add the same initialization:  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       public [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Boolean decompressUntilEOF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           this.decompressUntilEof = decompressUntilEOF;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           this.memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ensure it defaults to [0m[32m"unset"[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Rationale: Consistency across constructors ensures that if the user does not [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall the setter, the factory can fall back to the default limit.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Use a default cap in the `.Z` branch**  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Retain the previously introduced constant:  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   private static final int DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB = [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In the switch handling `.Z` streams, compute the effective limit:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mZ.equalsIgnoreCase[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int effectiveLimit = memoryLimitInKb > [0m[1;36m0[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ? memoryLimitInKb[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           : DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return new [0m[1;35mZCompressorInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39min, effectiveLimit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Rationale: Unchanged behavior for existing users [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefault cap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, while allowing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsumers to override via `setMemoryLimitInKb`.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve existing behavior and threading assumptions**  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The factory is typically used to build a new compressor stream per instance.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allowing a single mutable field does not affect stateless use cases.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Thread safety is unchanged: users should configure the factory before sharing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit across threads [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame as any other setter-based configuration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Testing and validation**  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run all existing unit and integration tests; no tests modify or reflect on [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memoryLimitInKb`, so none should break.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a small test in `CompressorStreamFactoryTest` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif not already present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat sets a tiny cap [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m KiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and verifies that decompressing a crafted “.Z” [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream exceeding the limit throws `MemoryLimitException`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validate that default behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithout setter[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still uses [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m MiB as intended.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is optimal:**  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It directly addresses the compile-time error by removing the incompatible `final`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifier.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It preserves all existing functionality and default resource usage.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It confines changes to a single class, avoiding impacts on other compressors or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness code.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It aligns with patterns used for other configurable parameters in the factory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `decompressUntilEof`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It reuses the already-introduced `DEFAULT_Z_MEMORY_LIMIT_IN_KB` constant, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimizing code churn.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mutable configuration may lead to unexpected caps if the same factory instance is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreused without resetting. Mitigate by documenting that `memoryLimitInKb` is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper-instance and advising users to create fresh instances for independent [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigurations.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to thread-safety guarantees beyond existing setter-based patterns.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStreamF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactory.jav[0m[1;92ma:430[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStreamF[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactory.jav[0m[1;92ma:550[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
